It is the perfect companion to students, hobbyists, and engineers.\r\n\r\nYou use it as you would any CAD program: you add elements, connect them together, and set their properties.\r\n\r\nBut iCircuit is unlike other CAD programs because it is always simulating. It's just like working with the real circuit. You do not stop to take a measurement or spend a lot of time configuring reports.
